22|1|ya eyyuhe-nnasu-tteku rabbekum. inne zelzelete-ssa`ati sey'un `azim
22|2|yevme teravneha tezhelu kullu murdi`atin `amma erda`at vetede`u kullu zati hamlin hamleha vetera-nnase sukara vema hum bisukara velakinne `azabe-llahi sedid
22|3|vemine-nnasi mey yucadilu fi-llahi bigayri `ilmiv veyettebi`u kulle seytanim merid
22|4|kutibe `aleyhi ennehu men tevellahu feennehu yudilluhu veyehdihi ila `azabi-sse`ir
22|5|ya eyyuhe-nnasu in kuntum fi raybim mine-lba`si feinna halaknakum min turabin summe min nutfetin summe min `alekatin summe mim mudgatim muhallekativ vegayri muhallekatil linubeyyine lekum. venukirru fi-l'erhami ma nesau ila ecelim musemmen summe nuhricukum tiflen summe liteblugu esuddekum. veminkum mey yuteveffa veminkum mey yuraddu ila erzeli-l`umuri likeyla ya`leme mim ba`di `ilmin sey'a. vetera-l'arda hamideten feiza enzelna `aleyhe-lmae-htezzet verabet veembetet min kulli zevcim behic
22|6|zalike bienne-llahe huve-lhakku veennehu yuhyi-lmevta veennehu `ala kulli sey'in kadir
22|7|veenne-ssa`ate atiyetul la raybe fiha veenne-llahe yeb`asu men fi-lkubur
22|8|vemine-nnasi mey yucadilu fi-llahi bigayri `ilmiv vela hudev vela kitabim munir
22|9|saniye `itfihi liyudille `an sebili-llah. lehu fi-ddunya hizyuv venuzikuhu yevme-lkiyameti `azabe-lharik
22|10|zalike bima kaddemet yedake veenne-llahe leyse bizallamil lil`abid
22|11|vemine-nnasi mey ya`budu-llahe `ala harf. fein esabehu hayrun-tmeenne bih. vein esabethu fitnetun-nkalebe `ala vechih. hasira-ddunya vel'ahirah. zalike huve-lhusranu-lmubin
22|12|yed`u min duni-llahi ma la yedurruhu vema la yenfe`uh. zalike huve-ddalalu-lbe`id
22|13|yed`u lemen darruhu akrabu min nef`ih. lebi'se-lmevla velebi'se-l`asir
22|14|inne-llahe yudhilu-llezine amenu ve`amilu-ssalihati cennatin tecri min tahtihe-l'enhar. inne-llahe yef`alu ma yurid
22|15|men kane yezunnu el ley yensurahu-llahu fi-ddunya vel'ahirati felyemdud bisebebin ile-ssemai summe liyakta` felyenzur hel yuzhibenne keyduhu ma yegiz
22|16|vekezalike enzelnahu ayatim beyyinativ veenne-llahe yehdi mey yurid
22|17|inne-llezine amenu vellezine hadu vessabi'ine vennesara velmecuse vellezine esraku. inne-llahe yefsilu beynehum yevme-lkiyameh. inne-llahe `ala kulli sey'in sehid
22|18|elem tera enne-llahe yescudu lehu men fi-ssemavati vemen fi-l'ardi vessemsu velkameru vennucumu velcibalu vesseceru veddevabbu vekesirum mine-nnas. vekesirun hakka `aleyhi-l`azab. vemey yuhini-llahu fema lehu mim mukrim. inne-llahe yef`alu ma yesa
22|19|hazani hasmani-htesamu fi rabbihim. fellezine keferu kutti`at lehum siyabum min narin. yusabbu min fevki ruusihimu-lhamim
22|20|yusheru bihi ma fi butunihim velculud
22|21|velehum mekami`u min hadid
22|22|kullema eradu ey yahrucu minha min gammin u`idu fiha vezuku `azabe-lharik
22|23|inne-llahe yudhilu-llezine amenu ve`amilu-ssalihati cennatin tecri min tahtihe-l'enharu yuhallevne fiha min esavira min zehebiv velu'lua. velibasuhum fiha harir
22|24|vehudu ile-ttayyibi mine-lkavl. vehudu ila sirati-lhamid
22|25|inne-llezine keferu veyesuddune `an sebili-llahi velmescidi-lharami-llezi ce`alnahu linnasi sevaeni-l`akifu fihi velbad. vemey yurid fihi biilhadim bizulmin nuzikhu min `azabin elim
22|26|veiz bevve'na liibrahime mekane-lbeyti el la tusrik bi sey'ev vetahhir beytiye littaifine velkaimine verrukke`i-ssucud
22|27|veezzin fi-nnasi bilhacci ye'tuke ricalev ve`ala kulli damiriy ye'tine min kulli feccin `amik
22|28|liyeshedu menafi`a lehum veyezkuru-sme-llahi fi eyyamim ma`lumatin `ala ma razekahum mim behimeti-l'en`am. fekulu minha veat`imu-lbaise-lfekir
22|29|summe liyakdu tefesehum velyufu nuzurahum velyettavvefu bilbeyti-l`atik
22|30|zalik. vemey yu`azzim hurumati-llahi fehuve hayrul lehu `inde rabbih. veuhillet lekumu-l'en`amu illa ma yutla `aleykum fectenibu-rricse mine-l'evsani vectenibu kavle-zzur
22|31|hunefae lillahi gayra musrikine bih. vemey yusrik billahi fekeennema harra mine-ssemai fetahtafuhu-ttayru ev tehvi bihi-rrihu fi mekanin sehik
22|32|zalik. vemey yu`azzim se`aira-llahi feinneha min takve-lkulub
22|33|lekum fiha menafi`u ila ecelim musemmen summe mehilluha ile-lbeyti-l`atik
22|34|velikulli ummetin ce`alna mensekel liyezkuru-sme-llahi `ala ma razekahum mim behimeti-l'en`am. feilahukum ilahuv vahidun felehu eslimu. vebessiri-lmuhbitin
22|35|ellezine iza zukira-llahu vecilet kulubuhum vessabirine `ala ma esabehum velmukimi-ssalati vemimma razaknahum yunfikun
22|36|velbudne ce`alnaha lekum min se`airi-llahi lekum fiha hayr. fezkuru-sme-llahi `aleyha savaff. feiza vecebet cunubuha fekulu minha veat`imu-lkani`a velmu`terr. kezalike sehharnaha lekum le`allekum teskurun
22|37|ley yenale-llahe luhumuha vela dimauha velakiy yenaluhu-ttakva minkum. kezalike sehharaha lekum litukebbiru-llahe `ala ma hedakum. vebessiri-lmuhsinin
22|38|inne-llahe yudafi`u `ani-llezine amenu. inne-llahe la yuhibbu kulle havvanin kefur
22|39|uzine lillezine yukatelune biennehum zulimu. veinne-llahe `ala nasrihim lekadir
22|40|ellezine uhricu min diyarihim bigayri hakkin illa ey yekulu rabbune-llah. velevla def`u-llahi-nnase ba`dahum biba`dil lehuddimet savami`u vebiye`uv vesalevatuv vemesacidu yuzkeru fihe-smu-llahi kesira. veleyensuranne-llahu mey yensuruh. inne-llahe lekaviyyun `aziz
22|41|ellezine im mekkennahum fi-l'ardi ekamu-ssalate veatevu-zzekate veemeru bilma`rufi venehev `ani-lmunker. velillahi `akibetu-l'umur
22|42|veiy yukezzibuke fekad kezzebet kablehum kavmu nuhiv ve`aduv vesemud
22|43|vekavmu ibrahime vekavmu lut
22|44|veashabu medyen. vekuzzibe musa feemleytu lilkafirine summe ehaztuhum. fekeyfe kane nekir
22|45|fekeeyyim min karyetin ehleknaha vehiye zalimetun fehiye haviyetun `ala `urusiha vebi'rim mu`attaletiv vekasrim mesid
22|46|efelem yesiru fi-l'ardi fetekune lehum kulubuy ya`kilune biha ev azanuy yesme`une biha. feinneha la ta`me-l'ebsaru velakin ta`me-lkulubu-lleti fi-ssudur
22|47|veyesta`ciluneke bil`azabi veley yuhlife-llahu va`deh. veinne yevmen `inde rabbike keelfi senetim mimma te`uddun
22|48|vekeeyyim min karyetin emleytu leha vehiye zalimetun summe ehaztuha. veileyye-lmesir
22|49|kul ya eyyuhe-nnasu innema ene lekum nezirum mubin
22|50|fellezine amenu ve`amilu-ssalihati lehum magfiratuv verizkun kerim
22|51|vellezine se`av fi ayatina mu`acizine ulaike ashabu-lcehim
22|52|vema erselna min kablike mir rasuliv vela nebiyyin illa iza temenna elka-sseytanu fi umniyyetih. feyensehu-llahu ma yulki-sseytanu summe yuhkimu-llahu ayatih. vellahu `alimun hakim
22|53|liyec`ale ma yulki-sseytanu fitnetel lillezine fi kulubihim meraduv velkasiyeti kulubuhum. veinne-zzalimine lefi sikakim be`id
22|54|veliya`leme-llezine utu-l`ilme ennehu-lhakku mir rabbike feyu'minu bihi fetuhbita lehu kulubuhum. veinne-llahe lehadi-llezine amenu ila siratim mustekim
22|55|vela yezalu-llezine keferu fi miryetim minhu hatta te'tiyehumu-ssa`atu bagteten ev ye'tiyehum `azabu yevmin `akim
22|56|elmulku yevmeizil lillah. yahkumu beynehum. fellezine amenu ve`amilu-ssalihati fi cennati-nne`im
22|57|vellezine keferu vekezzebu biayatina feulaike lehum `azabum muhin
22|58|vellezine haceru fi sebili-llahi summe kutilu ev matu leyerzukannehumu-llahu rizkan hasena. veinne-llahe lehuve hayru-rrazikin
22|59|leyudhilennehum mudhaley yerdavneh. veinne-llahe le`alimun halim
22|60|zalik. vemen `akabe bimisli ma `ukibe bihi summe bugiye `aleyhi leyensurannehu-llah. inne-llahe le`afuvvun gafur
22|61|zalike bienne-llahe yulicu-lleyle fi-nnehari veyulicu-nnehara fi-lleyli veenne-llahe semi`um besir
22|62|zalike bienne-llahe huve-lhakku veenne ma yed`une min dunihi huve-lbatilu veenne-llahe huve-l`aliyyu-lkebir
22|63|elem tera enne-llahe enzele mine-ssemai maa. fetusbihu-l'ardu muhdarrah. inne-llahe letifun habir
22|64|lehu ma fi-ssemavati vema fi-l'ard. veinne-llahe lehuve-lganiyyu-lhamid
22|65|elem tera enne-llahe sehhara lekum ma fi-l'ardi velfulke tecri fi-lbahri biemrih. veyumsiku-ssemae en teka`a `ale-l'ardi illa biiznih. inne-llahe binnasi leraufur rahim
22|66|vehuve-llezi ahyakum. summe yumitukum summe yuhyikum. inne-l'insane lekefur
22|67|likulli ummetin ce`alna menseken hum nasikuhu fela yunazi`anneke fi-l'emri ved`u ila rabbik. inneke le`ala hudem mustekim
22|68|vein cadeluke fekuli-llahu a`lemu bima ta`melun
22|69|allahu yahkumu beynekum yevme-lkiyameti fima kuntum fihi tahtelifun
22|70|elem ta`lem enne-llahe ya`lemu ma fi-ssemai vel'ard. inne zalike fi kitab. inne zalike `ale-llahi yesir
22|71|veya`budune min duni-llahi ma lem yunezzil bihi sultanev vema leyse lehum bihi `ilm. vema lizzalimine min nesir
22|72|veiza tutla `aleyhim ayatuna beyyinatin ta`rifu fi vucuhi-llezine keferu-lmunker. yekadune yestune billezine yetlune `aleyhim ayatina. kul efeunebbiukum biserrim min zalikum. ennar. ve`adehe-llahu-llezine keferu. vebi'se-lmesir

24|1|suratun enzelnaha veferadnaha veenzelna fiha ayatim beyyinatil le`allekum tezekkerun
24|2|ezzaniyetu vezzani feclidu kulle vahidim minhuma miete celdeh. vela te'huzkum bihima ra'fetun fi dini-llahi in kuntum tu'minune billahi velyevmi-l'ahir. velyeshed `azabehuma taifetum mine-lmu'minin
24|3|ezzani la yenkihu illa zaniyeten ev musrikeh. vezzaniyetu la yenkihuha illa zanin ev musrik. vehurrime zalike `ale-lmu'minin
24|4|vellezine yermune-lmuhsenati summe lem ye'tu bierbe`ati suhedae fecliduhum semanine celdetev vela takbelu lehum sehadeten ebeda. veulaike humu-lfasikun

24|9|velhamisete enne gadabe-llahi `aleyha in kane mine-ssadikin
24|10|velevla fadlu-llahi `aleykum verahmetuhu veenne-llahe tevvabun hakim
24|11|inne-llezine cau bil'ifki `usbetum minkum. la tahsebuhu serral lekum. bel huve hayrul lekum. likulli-mriim minhum me-ktesebe mine-l'ism. vellezi tevella kibrahu minhum lehu `azabun `azim
24|12|levla iz semi`tumuhu zanne-lmu'minune velmu'minatu bienfusihim hayrav vekalu haza ifkum mubin
24|13|levla cau `aleyhi bierbe`ati suheda'. feiz lem ye'tu bissuhedai feulaike `inde-llahi humu-lkazibun
24|14|velevla fadlu-llahi `aleykum verahmetuhu fi-ddunya vel'ahirati lemessekum fi ma efadtum fihi `azabun `azim
24|15|iz telekkavnehu bielsinetikum vetekulune biefvahikum ma leyse lekum bihi `ilmuv vetahsebunehu heyyina. vehuve `inde-llahi `azim
24|16|velevla iz semi`tumuhu kultum ma yekunu lena en netekelleme bihaza. subhaneke haza buhtanun `azim
24|17|ye`izukumu-llahu en te`udu limislihi ebeden in kuntum mu'minin
24|18|veyubeyyinu-llahu lekumu-l'ayat. vellahu `alimun hakim
24|19|inne-llezine yuhibbune en tesi`a-lfahisetu fi-llezine amenu lehum `azabun elimun fi-ddunya vel'ahirah. vellahu ya`lemu veentum la ta`lemun
24|20|velevla fadlu-llahi `aleykum verahmetuhu veenne-llahe raufur rahim
24|21|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu la tettebi`u hutuvati-sseytan. vemey yettebi` hutuvati-sseytani feinnehu ye'muru bilfahsai velmunker. velevla fadlu-llahi `aleykum verahmetuhu ma zeka minkum min ehadin ebedev velakinne-llahe yuzekki mey yesa'. vellahu semi`un `alim
24|22|vela ye'teli ulu-lfadli minkum vesse`ati ey yu'tu uli-lkurba velmesakine velmuhacirine fi sebili-llah. velya`fu velyasfehu. ela tuhibbune ey yagfira-llahu lekum. vellahu gafurur rahim
24|23|inne-llezine yermune-lmuhsenati-lgafilati-lmu'minati lu`inu fi-ddunya vel'ahirah. velehum `azabun `azim
24|24|yevme teshedu `aleyhim elsinetuhum veeydihim veerculuhum bima kanu ya`melun
24|25|yevmeiziy yuveffihimu-llahu dinehumu-lhakka veya`lemune enne-llahe huve-lhakku-lmubin
24|26|elhabisatu lilhabisine velhabisune lilhabisat. vettayyibatu littayyibine vettayyibune littayyibat. ulaike muberraune mimma yekulun. lehum magfiratuv verizkun kerim
24|27|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu la tedhulu buyuten gayra buyutikum hatta teste'nisu vetusellimu `ala ehliha. zalikum hayrul lekum le`allekum tezekkerun
24|28|feil lem tecidu fiha ehaden fela tedhuluha hatta yu'zene lekum. vein kile lekumu-rci`u ferci`u huve ezka lekum. vellahu bima ta`melune `alim
24|29|leyse `aleykum cunahun en tedhulu buyuten gayra meskunetin fiha meta`ul lekum. vellahu ya`lemu ma tubdune vema tektumun

24|31|vekul lilmu'minati yagdudne min ebsarihinne veyahfazne furucehunne vela yubdine zinetehunne illa ma zahera minha velyadribne bihumurihinne `ala cuyubihinn. vela yubdine zinetehunne illa libu`uletihinne ev abaihinne ev abai bu`uletihinne ev ebnaihinne ev ebnai bu`uletihinne ev ihvanihinne ev beni ihvanihinne ev beni ehavatihinne ev nisaihinne ev ma meleket eymanuhunne evi-ttabi`ine gayri uli-l'irbeti mine-rricali evi-ttifli-llezine lem yazheru `ala `avrati-nnisa'. vela yadribne bierculihinne liyu`leme ma yuhfine min zinetihinn. vetubu ile-llahi cemi`an eyyuhe-lmu'minune le`allekum tuflihun
24|32|venkihu-l'eyama minkum vessalihine min `ibadikum veimaikum. iy yekunu fukarae yugnihimu-llahu min fadlih. vellahu vasi`un `alim
24|33|velyesta`fifi-llezine la yecidune nikahan hatta yugniyehumu-llahu min fadlih. vellezine yebtegune-lkitabe mimma meleket eymanukum fekatibuhum in `alimtum fihim hayra. veatuhum mim mali-llahi-llezi atakum. vela tukrihu feteyatikum `ale-lbigai in eradne tehassunel litebtegu `arada-lhayati-ddunya. vemey yukrihhunne feinne-llahe mim ba`di ikrahihinne gafurur rahim
24|34|velekad enzelna ileykum ayatim mubeyyinativ vemeselem mine-llezine halev min kablikum vemev`izatel lilmuttekin
24|35|allahu nuru-ssemavati vel'ard. meselu nurihi kemiskatin fiha misbah. elmisbahu fi zucaceh. ezzucacetu keenneha kevkebun durriyyuy yukadu min seceratim mubaraketin zeytunetil la serkiyyetiv vela garbiyyetiy yekadu zeytuha yudiu velev lem temseshu narun. nurun `ala nur. yehdi-llahu linurihi mey yesa'. veyadribu-llahu-l'emsale linnas. vellahu bikulli sey'in `alim
24|36|fi buyutin ezine-llahu en turfe`a veyuzkera fihe-smuhu yusebbihu lehu fiha bilguduvvi vel'esal
24|37|ricalul la tulhihim ticaratuv vela bey`un `an zikri-llahi veikami-ssalati veitai-zzekati yehafune yevmen tetekallebu fihi-lkulubu vel'ebsar
24|38|liyecziyehumu-llahu ahsene ma `amilu veyezidehum min fadlih. vellahu yerzuku mey yesau bigayri hisab
24|39|vellezine keferu a`maluhum keserabim biki`atiy yahsebuhu-zzam'anu maa. hatta iza caehu lem yecidhu sey'ev vevecede-llahe `indehu feveffahu hisabeh. vellahu seri`u-lhisab
24|40|ev kezulumatin fi bahril lucciyyiy yagsahu mevcum min fevkihi mevcum min fevkihi sehab. zulumatum ba`duha fevka ba`d. iza ahrace yedehu lem yeked yeraha. vemel lem yec`ali-llahu lehu nuran fema lehu min nur
24|41|elem tera enne-llahe yusebbihu lehu men fi-ssemavati vel'ardi vettayru saffat. kullun kad `alime salatehu vetesbihah. vellahu `alimum bima yef`alun
24|42|velillahi mulku-ssemavati vel'ard. veile-llahi-lmesir
24|43|elem tera enne-llahe yuzci sehaben summe yu'ellifu beynehu summe yec`aluhu rukamen fetere-lvedka yahrucu min hilalih. veyunezzilu mine-ssemai min cibalin fiha mim beradin feyusibu bihi mey yesau veyasrifuhu `am mey yesa'. yekadu sena berkihi yezhebu bil'ebsar
24|44|yukallibu-llahu-lleyle vennehar. inne fi zalike le`ibratel liuli-l'ebsar
24|45|vellahu haleka kulle dabbetim mim ma'. feminhum mey yemsi `ala batnih. veminhum mey yemsi `ala ricleyn. veminhum mey yemsi `ala erba`. yahluku-llahu ma yesa'. inne-llahe `ala kulli sey'in kadir
24|46|lekad enzelna ayatim mubeyyinat. vellahu yehdi mey yesau ila siratim mustekim
24|47|veyekulune amenna billahi vebirrasuli veeta`na summe yetevella ferikum minhum mim ba`di zalik. vema ulaike bilmu'minin
24|48|veiza du`u ile-llahi verasulihi liyahkume beynehum iza ferikum minhum mu`ridun
24|49|veiy yekul lehumu-lhakku ye'tu ileyhi muz`inin
24|50|efi kulubihim meradun emi-rtabu em yehafune ey yehife-llahu `aleyhim verasuluh. bel ulaike humu-zzalimun
24|51|innema kane kavle-lmu'minine iza du`u ile-llahi verasulihi liyahkume beynehum ey yekulu semi`na veeta`na. veulaike humu-lmuflihun
24|52|vemey yuti`i-llahe verasulehu veyahse-llahe veyettakhi feulaike humu-lfaizun
24|53|veaksemu billahi cehde eymanihim lein emertehum leyahrucunn. kul la tuksimu. ta`atum ma`rufeh. inne-llahe habirum bima ta`melun
24|54|kul eti`u-llahe veeti`u-rrasul. fein tevellev feinnema `aleyhi ma hummile ve`aleykum ma hummiltum. vein tuti`uhu tehtedu. vema `ale-rrasuli ille-lbelagu-lmubin
24|55|ve`ade-llahu-llezine amenu minkum ve`amilu-ssalihati leyestahlifennehum fi-l'ardi keme-stahlefe-llezine min kablihim. veleyumekkinenne lehum dinehumu-llezi-rteda lehum veleyubeddilennehum mim ba`di havfihim emna. ya`buduneni la yusrikune bi sey'a. vemen kefera ba`de zalike feulaike humu-lfasikun
24|56|veekimu-ssalate veatu-zzekate veeti`u-rrasule le`allekum turhamun
24|57|la tahsebenne-llezine keferu mu`cizine fi-l'ard. veme'vahumu-nnar. velebi'se-lmesir
24|58|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu liyeste'zinkumu-llezine meleket eymanukum vellezine lem yeblugu-lhulume minkum selase merrat. min kabli salati-lfecri vehine teda`une siyabekum mine-zzahirati vemim ba`di salati-l`isa'. selasu `avratil lekum. leyse `aleykum vela `aleyhim cunahum ba`dehunn. tavvafune `aleykum ba`dukum `ala ba`d. kezalike yubeyyinu-llahu lekumu-l'ayat. vellahu `alimun hakim
24|59|veiza belega-l'atfalu minkumu-lhulume felyeste'zinu keme-ste'zene-llezine min kablihim. kezalike yubeyyinu-llahu lekum ayatih. vellahu `alimun hakim
24|60|velkava`idu mine-nnisai-llati la yercune nikahan feleyse `aleyhinne cunahun ey yeda`ne siyabehunne gayra muteberricatim bizineh. veey yesta`fifne hayrul lehunn. vellahu semi`un `alim
24|61|leyse `ale-l'a`ma haracuv vela `ale-l'a`raci haracuv vela `ale-lmeridi haracuv vela `ala enfusikum en te'kulu mim buyutikum ev buyuti abaikum ev buyuti ummehatikum ev buyuti ihvanikum ev buyuti ehavatikum ev buyuti a`mamikum ev buyuti `ammatikum ev buyuti ahvalikum ev buyuti halatikum ev ma melektum mefatihahu ev sadikikum. leyse `aleykum cunahun en te'kulu cemi`an ev estata. feiza dehaltum buyuten fesellimu `ala enfusikum tehiyyetem min `indi-llahi mubaraketen tayyibeh. kezalike yubeyyinu-llahu lekumu-l'ayati le`allekum ta`kilun
24|62|inneme-lmu'minune-llezine amenu billahi verasulihi veiza kanu me`ahu `ala emrin cami`il lem yezhebu hatta yeste'zinuh. inne-llezine yeste'zinuneke ulaike-llezine yu'minune billahi verasulih. feize-ste'zenuke liba`di se'nihim fe'zel limen si'te minhum vestagfir lehumu-llah. inne-llahe gafurur rahim
24|63|la tec`alu du`ae-rrasuli beynekum kedu`ai ba`dikum ba`da. kad ya`lemu-llahu-llezine yetesellelune minkum livaza. felyahzeri-llezine yuhalifune `an emrih en tusibehum fitnetun ev yusibehum `azabun elim
24|64|ela inne lillahi ma fi-ssemavati vel'ard. kad ya`lemu ma entum `aleyh. veyevme yurce`une ileyhi feyunebbiuhum bima `amilu. vellahu bikulli sey'in `alim
25|1|tebarake-llezi nezzele-lfurkane `ala `abdihi liyekune lil`alemine nezira
25|2|ellezi lehu mulku-ssemavati vel'ardi velem yettehiz veledev velem yekul lehu serikun fi-lmulki vehaleka kulle sey'in fekadderahu takdira
25|3|vettehazu min dunihi alihetel la yahlukune sey'ev vehum yuhlekune vela yemlikune lienfusihim darrav vela nef`av vela yemlikune mevtev vela hayatev vela nusura
25|4|vekale-llezine keferu in haza illa ifkun-fterahu vee`anehu `aleyhi kavmun aharun. fekad cau zulmev vezura
25|5|vekalu esatiru-l'evveline-ktetebeha fehiye tumla `aleyhi bukratev veesila

25|7|vekalu ma lihaze-rrasuli ye'kulu-tta`ame veyemsi fi-l'esvak. levla unzile ileyhi melekun feyekune me`ahu nezira

28|8|feltekatahu alu fir`avne liyekune lehum `aduvvev vehazena. inne fir`avne vehamane vecunudehuma kanu hatiin

28|15|vedehale-lmedinete `ala hini gafletim min ehliha fevecede fiha raculeyni yaktetilan. haza min si`atihi vehaza min `aduvvih. festegasehu-llezi min si`atihi `ale-llezi min `aduvvihi fevekezehu musa fekada `aleyh. kale haza min `ameli-sseytan. innehu `aduvvum mudillum mubin
28|16|kale rabbi inni zalemtu nefsi fagfir li fegafera leh. innehu huve-lgafuru-rrahim

28|19|felemma en erade ey yebtise billezi huve `aduvvul lehuma kale ya musa eturidu en taktuleni kema katelte nefsem bil'ems. in turidu illa en tekune cebbaran fi-l'ardi vema turidu en tekune mine-lmuslihin

28|25|fecaethu ihdahuma temsi `ale-stihya'. kalet inne ebi yed`uke liyecziyeke ecra ma sekayte lena. felemma caehu vekassa `aleyhi-lkasasa kale la tehaf. necevte mine-lkavmi-zzalimin
28|26|kalet ihdahuma ya ebeti-ste'cirh. inne hayra meni-ste'certe-lkaviyyu-l'emin
28|27|kale inni uridu en unkihake ihde-bneteyye hateyni `ala en te'curani semaniye hicec. fein etmemte `asran femin `indik. vema uridu en esukka `aleyk. seteciduni in sae-llahu mine-ssalihin
28|28|kale zalike beyni vebeynek. eyyeme-l'eceleyni kadaytu fela `udvane `aleyy. vellahu `ala ma nekulu vekil

28|30|felemma etaha nudiye min satii-lvadi-l'eymeni fi-lbuk`ati-lmubaraketi mine-ssecerati ey ya musa inni ene-llahu rabbu-l`alemin

28|32|usluk yedeke fi ceybike tahruc beydae min gayri su'. vadmum ileyke cenahake mine-rrahbi fezanike burhanani mir rabbike ila fir`avne vemeleih. innehum kanu kavmen fasikin
28|33|kale rabbi inni kateltu minhum nefsen feehafu ey yaktulun

28|35|kale senesuddu `adudeke biehike venec`alu lekuma sultanen fela yesilune ileykuma biayatina. entuma vemeni-ttebe`akume-lgalibun
28|36|felemma caehum musa biayatina beyyinatin kalu ma haza illa sihrum mufterav vema semi`na bihaza fi abaine-l'evvelin
28|37|vekale musa rabbi a`lemu bimen cae bilhuda min `indihi vemen tekunu lehu `akibetu-ddar. innehu la yuflihu-zzalimun
28|38|vekale fir`avnu ya eyyuhe-lmeleu ma `alimtu lekum min ilahin gayri. feevkid li ya hamanu `ale-ttini fec`al li sarhal le`alli ettali`u ila ilahi musa veinni leezunnuhu mine-lkazibin
28|39|vestekbera huve vecunuduhu fi-l'ardi bigayri-lhakki vezannu ennehum ileyna la yurce`un
28|40|feehaznahu vecunudehu fenebeznahum fi-lyemm. fenzur keyfe kane `akibetu-zzalimin
28|41|vece`alnahum eimmetey yed`une ile-nnar. veyevme-lkiyameti la yunsarun
28|42|veetba`nahum fi hazihi-ddunya la`neten. veyevme-lkiyameti hum mine-lmakbuhin
28|43|velekad ateyna muse-lkitabe mim ba`di ma ehlekne-lkurune-l'ula besaira linnasi vehudev verahmetel le`allehum yetezekkerun
28|44|vema kunte bicanibi-lgarbiyyi iz kadayna ila muse-l'emra vema kunte mine-ssahidin
28|45|velakinna ense'na kurunen fetetavele `aleyhimu-l`umur. vema kunte saviyen fi ehli medyene tetlu `aleyhim ayatina velakinna kunna mursilin
28|46|vema kunte bicanibi-tturi iz nadeyna velakir rahmetem mir rabbike litunzira kavmem ma etahum min nezirim min kablike le`allehum yetezekkerun
28|47|velevla en tusibehum musibetum bima kaddemet eydihim feyekulu rabbena levla erselte ileyna rasulen fenettebi`a ayatike venekune mine-lmu'minin
28|48|felemma caehumu-lhakku min `indina kalu levla utiye misle ma utiye musa. evelem yekfuru bima utiye musa min kabl. kalu sihrani tezahera. vekalu inna bikullin kafirun
28|49|kul fe'tu bikitabim min `indi-llahi huve ehda minhuma ettebi`hu in kuntum sadikin
28|50|feil lem yestecibu leke fa`lem ennema yettebi`une ehvaehum. vemen edallu mimmeni-ttebe`a hevahu bigayri hudem mine-llah. inne-llahe la yehdi-lkavme-zzalimin
28|51|velekad vessalna lehumu-lkavle le`allehum yetezekkerun
28|52|ellezine ateynahumu-lkitabe min kablihi hum bihi yu'minun
28|53|veiza yutla `aleyhim kalu amenna bihi innehu-lhakku mir rabbina inna kunna min kablihi muslimin
28|54|ulaike yu'tevne ecrahum merrateyni bima saberu veyedraune bilhaseneti-sseyyiete vemimma razaknahum yunfikun
28|55|veiza semi`u-llagve a`radu `anhu vekalu lena a`maluna velekum a`malukum. selamun `aleykum. la nebtegi-lcahilin
28|56|inneke la tehdi men ahbebte velakinne-llahe yehdi mey yesa'. vehuve a`lemu bilmuhtedin
28|57|vekalu in nettebi`i-lhuda me`ake nutehattef min ardina. evelem numekkil lehum haramen aminey yucba ileyhi semeratu kulli sey'ir rizkam mil ledunna velakinne ekserahum la ya`lemun
28|58|vekem ehlekna min karyetim betirat me`iseteha. fetilke mesakinuhum lem tuskem mim ba`dihim illa kalila. vekunna nahnu-lvarisin
28|59|vema kane rabbuke muhlike-lkura hatta yeb`ase fi ummiha rasuley yetlu `aleyhim ayatina. vema kunna muhliki-lkura illa veehluha zalimun
28|60|vema utitum min sey'in femeta`u-lhayati-ddunya vezinetuha. vema `inde-llahi hayruv veebka. efela ta`kilun
28|61|efemev ve`adnahu va`den hasenen fehuve lakihi kemem metta`nahu meta`a-lhayati-ddunya summe huve yevme-lkiyameti mine-lmuhdarin
28|62|veyevme yunadihim feyekulu eyne surakaiye-llezine kuntum tez`umun

28|64|vekile-d`u surakaekum fede`avhum felem yestecibu lehum veraevu-l`azab. lev ennehum kanu yehtedun
28|65|veyevme yunadihim feyekulu maza ecebtumu-lmurselin
28|66|fe`amiyet `aleyhimu-l'embau yevmeizin fehum la yetesaelun

28|68|verabbuke yahluku ma yesau veyahtar. ma kane lehumu-lhiyerah. subhane-llahi vete`ala `amma yusrikun
28|69|verabbuke ya`lemu ma tukinnu suduruhum vema yu`linun
28|70|vehuve-llahu la ilahe illa hu. lehu-lhamdu fi-l'ula vel'ahirah. velehu-lhukmu veileyhi turce`un
28|71|kul era'eytum in ce`ale-llahu `aleykumu-lleyle sermeden ila yevmi-lkiyameti men ilahun gayru-llahi ye'tikum bidiya'. efela tesme`un
28|72|kul era'eytum in ce`ale-llahu `aleykumu-nnehara sermeden ila yevmi-lkiyameti men ilahun gayru-llahi ye'tikum bileylin teskunune fih. efela tubsirun
28|73|vemir rahmetihi ce`ale lekumu-lleyle vennehara liteskunu fihi velitebtegu min fadlihi vele`allekum teskurun
28|74|veyevme yunadihim feyekulu eyne surakaiye-llezine kuntum tez`umun
28|75|veneza`na min kulli ummetin sehiden fekulna hatu burhanekum fe`alimu enne-lhakka lillahi vedalle `anhum ma kanu yefterun
28|76|inne karune kane min kavmi musa febega `aleyhim. veateynahu mine-lkunuzi ma inne mefatihahu letenuu bil`usbeti uli-lkuvveh. iz kale lehu kavmuhu la tefrah inne-llahe la yuhibbu-lferihin
28|77|vebtegi fima atake-llahu-ddara-l'ahirate vela tense nesibeke mine-ddunya veahsin kema ahsene-llahu ileyke vela tebgi-lfesade fi-l'ard. inne-llahe la yuhibbu-lmufsidin
28|78|kale innema utituhu `ala `ilmin `indi. evelem ya`lem enne-llahe kad ehleke min kablihi mine-lkuruni men huve eseddu minhu kuvvetev veekseru cem`a. vela yus'elu `an zunubihimu-lmucrimun
28|79|feharace `ala kavmihi fi zinetih. kale-llezine yuridune-lhayate-ddunya ya leyte lena misle ma utiye karunu innehu lezu hazzin `azim
28|80|vekale-llezine utu-l`ilme veylekum sevabu-llahi hayrul limen amene ve`amile saliha. vela yulekkaha ille-ssabirun
28|81|fehasefna bihi vebidarihi-l'arda fema kane lehu min fietiy yensurunehu min duni-llah. vema kane mine-lmuntesirin
28|82|veasbeha-llezine temennev mekanehu bil'emsi yekulune veykeenne-llahe yebsutu-rrizka limey yesau min `ibadihi veyakdir. levla em menne-llahu `aleyna lehasefe bina. veykeennehu la yuflihu-lkafirun
28|83|tilke-ddaru-l'ahiratu nec`aluha lillezine la yuridune `uluvven fi-l'ardi vela fesada. vel`akibetu lilmuttekin

29|1|elif-lam-mim
29|2|ehasibe-nnasu ey yutraku ey yekulu amenna vehum la yuftenun
29|3|velekad fetenne-llezine min kablihim feleya`lemenne-llahu-llezine sadeku veleya`lemenne-lkazibin
29|4|em hasibe-llezine ya`melune-sseyyiati ey yesbikuna. sae ma yahkumun
29|5|men kane yercu likae-llahi feinne ecele-llahi leatin. vehuve-ssemi`u-l`alim
29|6|vemen cahede feinnema yucahidu linefsih. inne-llahe leganiyyun `ani-l`alemin
29|7|vellezine amenu ve`amilu-ssalihati lenukeffiranne `anhum seyyiatihim velenecziyennehum ahsene-llezi kanu ya`melun
29|8|vevessayne-l'insane bivalideyhi husna. vein cahedake litusrike bi ma leyse leke bihi `ilmun fela tuti`huma. ileyye merci`ukum feunebbiukum bima kuntum ta`melun
29|9|vellezine amenu ve`amilu-ssalihati lenudhilennehum fi-ssalihin
29|10|vemine-nnasi mey yekulu amenna billahi feiza uziye fi-llahi ce`ale fitnete-nnasi ke`azabi-llah. velein cae nasrum mir rabbike leyekulunne inna kunna me`akum. eveleyse-llahu bia`leme bima fi suduri-l`alemin
29|11|veleya`lemenne-llahu-llezine amenu veleya`lemenne-lmunafikin
29|12|vekale-llezine keferu lillezine amenu-ttebi`u sebilena velnahmil hatayakum. vema hum bihamiline min hatayahum min sey'. innehum lekazibun
29|13|veleyahmilunne eskalehum eskalem me`a eskalekum. veleyus'elunne yevme-lkiyameti `amma kanu yefterun

29|15|feenceynahu veashabe-ssefineti vece`alnaha ayetel lil`alemin
29|16|veibrahime iz kale likavmihi-`budu-llahe vettekuh. zalikum hayrul lekum in kuntum ta`lemun
29|17|innema ta`budune min duni-llahi evsanev vetahlukune ifka. inne-llezine ta`budune min duni-llahi la yemlikune lekum rizkan febtegu `inde-llahi-rrizka va`buduhu veskuru leh. ileyhi turce`un
29|18|vein tukezzibu fekad kezzebe umemum min kablikum. vema `ale-rrasuli ille-lbelagu-lmubin

29|20|kul siru fi-l'ardi fenzuru keyfe bedee-lhalka summe-llahu yunsiu-nnes'ete-l'ahirah. inne-llahe `ala kulli sey'in kadir
29|21|yu`azzibu mey yesau veyerhamu mey yesa'. veileyhi tuklebun
29|22|vema entum bimu`cizine fi-l'ardi vela fi-ssema'. vema lekum min duni-llahi miv veliyyiv vela nesir
29|23|vellezine keferu biayati-llahi velikaihi ulaike yeisu mir rahmeti veulaike lehum `azabun elim
29|24|fema kane cevabe kavmihi illa en kalu-ktuluhu ev harrikuhu feencahu-llahu mine-nnar. inne fi zalike leayatil likavmiy yu'minun
29|25|vekale inneme-ttehaztum min duni-llahi evsanem meveddete beynikum fi-lhayati-ddunya. summe yevme-lkiyameti yekfuru ba`dukum biba`div veyel`anu ba`dukum ba`da. veme'vakum-nnaru vema lekum min nasirin
29|26|feamene lehu lut. vekale inni muhacirun ila rabbi. innehu huve-l`azizu-lhakim
29|27|vevehebna lehu ishaka veya`kube vece`alna fi zurriyyetehu-nnubuvvete velkitabe veateynahu ecrahu fi-ddunya. veinnehu fi-l'ahirati lemine-ssalihin
29|28|velutan iz kale likavmihi innekum lete'tune-lfahiseh. ma sebekakum biha min ehadim mine-l`alemin
29|29|einnekum lete'tune-rricale vetakta`une-ssebile vete'tune fi nadikumu-lmunker. fema kane cevabe kavmihi illa en kalu-'tina bi`azabi-llahi in kunte mine-ssadikin
29|30|kale rabbi-nsurni `ale-lkavmi-lmufsidin

29|32|kale inne fiha luta. kalu nahnu a`lemu bimen fiha. lenunecciyennehu veehlehu ille-mraeteh. kanet mine-lgabirin
29|33|velemma en caet rusuluna lutan sie bihim vedaka bihim zer`av vekalu la tehaf vela tahzen. inna muneccuke veehleke ille-mraeteke kanet mine-lgabirin
29|34|inna munzilune `ala ehli hazihi-lkaryeti riczem mine-ssemai bima kanu yefsukun

29|40|fekullen ehazna bizembih. feminhum men erselna `aleyhi hasiba. veminhum men ehazethu-ssayhah. veminhum men hasefna bihi-l'ard. veminhum men agrakna. vema kane-llahu liyazlimehum velakin kanu enfusehum yazlimun
29|41|meselu-llezine-ttehazu min duni-llahi evliyae kemeseli-l`nkebut. ittehazet beyta. veinne evhene-lbuyuti lebeytu-l`nkebut. lev kanu ya`lemun
29|42|inne-llahe ya`lemu ma yed`une min dunihi min sey'. vehuve-l`azizu-lhakim

29|44|haleka-llahu-ssemavati vel'arda bilhakk. inne fi zalike leayetel lilmu'minin
29|45|utlu ma uhiye ileyke mine-lkitabi veekimi-ssalah. inne-ssalate tenha `ani-lfahsai velmunker. velezikru-llahi ekber. vellahu ya`lemu ma tasne`un
29|46|vela tucadilu ehle-lkitabi illa billeti hiye ahsen. ille-llezine zalemu minhum vekulu amenna billezi unzile ileyna veunzile ileykum veileyha veilahukum vahiduv venahnu lehu muslimun
29|47|vekezalike enzelna ileyke-lkitab. fellezine ateynahumu-lkitabe yu'minune bih. vemin haulai mey yu'minu bih. vema yechadu biayatina ille-lkafirun
29|48|vema kunte tetlu min kablihi min kitabiv vela tehuttuhu biyeminike izel lertabe-lmubtilun
29|49|bel huve ayatum beyyinatun fi suduri-llezine utu-l`ilm. vema yechadu biayatina ille-zzalimun
29|50|vekalu levla unzile `aleyhi ayatum mir rabbih. kul inneme-l'ayatu `inde-llah. veinnema ene nezirum mubin
29|51|evelem yekfihim enna enzelna `aleyke-lkitabe yutla `aleyhim. inne fi zalike lerahmetev vezikra likavmiy yu'minun
29|52|kul kefa billahi beyni vebeynekum sehida. ya`lemu ma fi-ssemavati vel'ard. vellezine amenu bilbatili vekeferu billahi ulaike humu-lhasirun

29|54|yesta`ciluneke bil`azab. veinne cehenneme lemuhitatum bilkafirin

29|63|velein seeltehum men nezzele mine-ssemai maen feahya bihi-l'arda mim ba`di mevtiha leyekulunne-llah. kuli-lhamdu lillah. bel ekseruhum la ya`kilun
29|64|vema hazihi-lhayatu-ddunya illa lehvuv vele`ib. veinne-ddara-l'ahirate lehiye-lhayevan. lev kanu ya`lemun

30|6|va`de-llah. la yuhlifu-llahu va`dehu velakinne eksera-nnasi la ya`lemun
30|7|ya`lemune zahiram mine-lhayati-ddunya. vehum `ani-l'ahirati hum gafilun
30|8|evelem yetefekkeru fi enfusihim. ma haleka-llahu-ssemavati vel'arda vema beynehuma illa bilhakki veecelim musemma. veinne kesiram mine-nnasi bilikai rabbihim lekafirun
30|9|evelem yesiru fi-l'ardi feyenzuru keyfe kane `akibetu-llezine min kablihim. kanu esedde minhum kuvvetev veesaru-l'arda ve`ameruha eksera mimma `ameruha vecaethum rusuluhum bilbeyyinat. fema kane-llahu liyazlimehum velakin kanu enfusehum yazlimun

30|21|vemin ayatihi en haleka lekum min enfusikum ezvacel liteskunu ileyha vece`ale beynekum meveddetev verahmeh. inne fi zalike leayatil likavmiy yetefekkerun
30|22|vemin ayatihi halku-ssemavati vel'ardi vahtilafu elsinetikum veelvanikum. inne fi zalike leayatil lil'`alimin
30|23|vemin ayatihi menamukum billeyli vennehari vebtigaukum min fadlih. inne fi zalike leayatil likavmiy yesme`un
30|24|vemin ayatihi yurikumu-lberka havfev vetame`av veyunezzilu mine-ssemai maen feyuhyi bihi-l'arda ba`de mevtiha. inne fi zalike leayatil likavmiy ya`kilun
30|25|vemin ayatihi en tekume-ssemau vel'ardu biemrih. summe iza de`akum da`vetem mine-l'ardi iza entum tuhracun
30|26|velehu men fi-ssemavati vel'ard. kullul lehu kanitun
30|27|vehuve-llezi yebdeu-lhalka summe yu`iduhu vehuve ehvenu `aleyh. velehu-lmeselu-l'a`la fi-ssemavati vel'ard. vehuve-l`azizu-lhakim
30|28|darabe lekum meselem min enfusikum. hel lekum mim ma meleket eymanukum min surakae fi ma razaknakum feentum fihi sevaun tehafunehum kehifetikum enfusekum. kezalike nufessilu-l'ayati likavmiy ya`kilun
30|29|beli-ttebe`a-llezine zalemu ehvaehum bigayri `ilmin. femey yehdi men edalle-llah. vema lehum min nasirin
30|30|feekim vecheke lildini hanifa. fitrate-llahi-lleti fetara-nnase `aleyha. la tebdile lihalki-llah. zalike-ddinu-lkayyim. velakinne eksera-nnasi la ya`lemun
30|31|munibine ileyhi vettekuhu veekimu-ssalate vela tekunu mine-lmusrikin
30|32|mine-llezine ferraku dinehum vekanu siye`a. kullu hizbim bima ledeyhim ferihun
30|33|veiza messe-nnase durrun de`av rabbehum munibine ileyhi summe iza ezakahum minhu rahmeten iza ferikum minhum birabbihim yusrikun
30|34|liyekfuru bima ateynahum. fetemette`u. fesevfe ta`lemun
30|35|em enzelna `aleyhim sultanen fehuve yetekellemu bima kanu bihi yusrikun
30|36|veiza ezakne-nnase rahmeten ferihu biha. vein tusibhum seyyietum bima kaddemet eydihim iza hum yaknetun
30|37|evelem yerav enne-llahe yebsutu-rrizka limey yesau veyakdir. inne fi zalike leayatil likavmiy yu'minun
30|38|feati ze-lkurba hakkahu velmiskine vebne-ssebil. zalike hayrul lillezine yuridune veche-llah. veulaike humu-lmuflihun
30|39|vema ateytum mir ribel liyerbuve fi emvali-nnasi fela yerbu `inde-llah. vema ateytum min zekatin turidune veche-llahi feulaike humu-lmud`ifun
30|40|allahu-llezi halekakum summe razekakum summe yumitukum summe yuhyikum. hel min surakaikum mey yef`alu min zalikum min sey'. subhanehu vete`ala `amma yusrikun
30|41|zahera-lfesadu fi-lberri velbahri bima kesebet eydi-nnasi liyuzikahum ba`da-llezi `amilu le`allehum yerci`un
30|42|kul siru fi-l'ardi fenzuru keyfe kane `akibetu-llezine min kabl. kane ekseruhum musrikin
30|43|feekim vecheke lildini-lkayyimi min kabli ey ye'tiye yevmul la meradde lehu mine-llahi yevmeiziy yessadde`un

33|53|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu la tedhulu buyute-nnebiyyi illa ey yu'zene lekum ila ta`amin gayra nazirine inahu velakin iza du`itum fedhulu feiza ta`imtum fentesiru vela muste'nisine lihadis. inne zalikum kane yu'zi-nnebiyye feyestahyi minkum. vellahu la yestahyi mine-lhakk. veiza seeltumuhunne meta`an fes'eluhunne miv verai hicab. zalikum atheru likulubikum vekulubihinn. vema kane lekum en tu'zu rasule-llahi vela en tenkihu ezvacehu mim ba`dihi ebeda. inne zalikum kane `inde-llahi `azima
33|54|in tubdu sey'en ev tuhfuhu feinne-llahe kane bikulli sey'in `alima

33|56|inne-llahe vemelaiketehu yusallune `ale-nnebiyy. ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu sallu `aleyhi vesellimu teslima

34|1|elhamdu lillahi-llezi lehu ma fi-ssemavati vema fi-l'ardi velehu-lhamdu fi-l'ahirah. vehuve-lhakimu-lhabir

34|3|vekale-llezine keferu la te'tine-ssa`ah. kul bela verabbi lete'tiyennekum `alimi-lgaybi. la ya`zubu `anhu miskalu zerratin fi-ssemavati vela fi-l'ardi vela asgaru min zalike vela ekberu illa fi kitabim mubin
34|4|liyecziye-llezine amenu ve`amilu-ssalihati. ulaike lehum magfiratuv verizkun kerim

34|13|ya`melune lehu ma yesau mim meharibe vetemasile vecifanin kelcevabi vekudurir rasiyat. i`melu ale davude sukra. vekalilum min `ibadiye-ssekur
34|14|felemma kadayna `aleyhi-lmevte ma dellehum `ala mevtih illa dabbetu-l'ardi te'kulu minseeteh. felemma harra tebeyyeneti-lcinnu el lev kanu ya`lemune-lgaybe ma lebisu fi-l`azabi-lmuhin
34|15|lekad kane lisebein fi meskenihim ayeh. cennetani `ay yeminiv vesimal. kulu mir rizki rabbikum veskuru leh. beldetun tayyibetuv verabbun gafur

34|23|vela tenfe`u-ssefa`atu `indehu illa limen ezine leh. hatta iza fuzzi`a `an kulubihim kalu maza kale rabbukum. kalu-lhakk. vehuve-l`aliyyu-lkebir

34|38|vellezine yes`avne fi ayatina mu`acizine ulaike fi-l`azabi muhdarun

35|1|elhamdu lillahi fatiri-ssemavati vel'ardi ca`ili-lmelaiketi rusulen uli ecnihatim mesna vesulase veruba`. yezidu fi-lhalki ma yesa'. inne-llahe `ala kulli sey'in kadir

39|1|tenzilu-lkitabi mine-llahi-l`azizi-lhakim
39|2|inna enzelna ileyke-lkitabe bilhakki fa`budi-llahe muhlisal lehu-ddin
39|3|ela lillahi-ddinu-lhalis. vellezine-ttehazu min dunihi evliya'. ma na`buduhum illa liyukarribuna ile-llahi zulfa. inne-llahe yahkumu beynehum fi ma hum fihi yahtelifun. inne-llahe la yehdi men huve kazibun keffar
39|4|lev erade-llahu ey yettehize veledel lastafa mimma yahluku ma yesau subhaneh. huve-llahu-lvahidu-lkahhar
39|5|haleka-ssemavati vel'arda bilhakk. yukevviru-lleyle `ale-nnehari veyukevviru-nnehara `ale-lleyli vesehhara-ssemse velkamer. kulluy yecri liecelim musemma. ela huve-l`azizu-lgaffar
39|6|halekakum min nefsiv vahidetin summe ce`ale minha zevceha veenzele lekum mine-l'en`ami semaniyete ezvac. yahlukukum fi butuni ummehatikum halkam mim ba`di halkin fi zulumatin selas. zalikumu-llahu rabbukum lehu-lmulk. la ilahe illa hu. feenna tusrafun
39|7|in tekfuru feinne-llahe ganiyyun `ankum vela yerda li`ibadihi-lkufr. vein teskuru yerdahu lekum. vela teziru vaziratuv vizra uhra. summe ila rabbikum merci`ukum feyunebbiukum bima kuntum ta`melun. innehu `alimum bizati-ssudur
39|8|veiza messe-l'insane durrun de`a rabbehu muniben ileyhi summe iza havvelehu ni`metem minhu nesiye ma kane yed`u ileyhi min kablu vece`ale lillahi endadel liyudille `an sebilih. kul temetta` bikufrike kalilen. inneke min ashabi-nnar
39|9|emmen huve kanitun anae-lleyli sacidev vekaimey yahzeru-l'ahirate veyercu rahmete rabbih. kul hel yestevi-llezine ya`lemune vellezine la ya`lemun. innema yetezekkeru ulu-l'elbab
39|10|kul ya `ibadi-llezine amenu-tteku rabbekum. lillezine ahsenu fi hazihi-ddunya haseneh. veardu-llahi vasi`ah. innema yuveffe-ssabirune ecrahum bigayri hisab

48|9|litu'minu billahi verasulihi vetu`azziruhu vetuvekkiruh. vetusebbihuhu bukratev veesila
48|10|inne-llezine yubayi`uneke innema yubayi`une-llah. yedu-llahi fevka eydihim. femen nekese feinnema yenkusu `ala nefsih. vemen evfa bima `ahede `aleyhu-llahe feseyu'tihi ecran `azima
48|11|seyekulu leke-lmuhallefune mine-l'a`rabi segaletna emvaluna veehluna festagfir lena. yekulune bielsinetihim ma leyse fi kulubihim. kul femey yemliku lekum mine-llahi sey'en in erade bikum darran ev erade bikum nef`a. bel kane-llahu bima ta`melune habira
48|12|bel zanentum el ley yenkalibe-rrasulu velmu'minune ila ehlihim ebedev vezuyyine zalike fi kulubikum vezanentum zanne-ssev'. vekuntum kavmem bura
48|13|vemel lem yu'mim billahi verasulihi feinna a`tedna lilkafirine se`ira
48|14|velillahi mulku-ssemavati vel'ard. yagfiru limey yesau veyu`azzibu mey yesa'. vekane-llahu gafurar rahima
48|15|seyekulu-lmuhallefune ize-ntalaktum ila meganime lite'huzuha zeruna nettebi`kum. yuridune ey yubeddilu kelame-llah. kul len tettebi`una kezalikum kale-llahu min kabl. feseyekulune bel tahsudunena. bel kanu la yefkahune illa kalila
48|16|kul lilmuhallefine mine-l'a`rabi setud`avne ila kavmin uli be'sin sedidin tukatilunehum ev yuslimun. fein tuti`u yu'tikumu-llahu ecran hasena. vein tetevellev kema tevelleytum min kablu yu`azzibkum `azaben elima
48|17|leyse `ale-l'a`ma haracuv vela `ale-l'a`raci haracuv vela `ale-lmeridi harac. vemey yuti`i-llahe verasulehu yudhilhu cennatin tecri min tahtihe-l'enhar. vemey yetevelle yu`azzibhu `azaben elima
48|18|lekad radiye-llahu `ani-lmu'minine iz yubayi`uneke tahte-ssecerati fe`alime ma fi kulubihim feenzele-ssekinete `aleyhim veesabehum fethan kariba
48|19|vemeganime kesiratey ye'huzuneha. vekane-llahu `azizen hakima
48|20|ve`adekumu-llahu meganime kesiraten te'huzuneha fe`accele lekum hazihi vekeffe eydiye-nnasi `ankum. velitekune ayetel lilmu'minine veyehdiyekum siratam mustekima
48|21|veuhra lem takdiru `aleyha kad ehata-llahu biha. vekane-llahu `ala kulli sey'in kadira
48|22|velev katelekumu-llezine keferu levellevu-l'edbara summe la yecidune veliyyev vela nesira
48|23|sunnete-llahi-lleti kad halet min kabl. velen tecide lisunneti-llahi tebdila
48|24|vehuve-llezi keffe eydiyehum `ankum veeydiyekum `anhum bibatni mekkete mim ba`di en azferakum `aleyhim. vekane-llahu bima ta`melune besira
48|25|humu-llezine keferu vesaddukum `ani-lmescidi-lharami velhedye ma`kufen ey yebluga mehilleh. velevla ricalum mu'minune venisaum mu'minatul lem ta`lemuhum en tetauhum fetusibekum minhum me`arratum bigayri `ilmin. liyudhile-llahu fi rahmetihi mey yesa'. lev tezeyyelu le`azzebne-llezine keferu minhum `azaben elima
48|26|iz ce`ale-llezine keferu fi kulubihimu-lhamiyyete hamiyyete-lcahiliyyeti feenzele-llahu sekinetehu `ala rasulihi ve`ale-lmu'minine veelzemehum kelimete-ttakva vekanu ehakka biha veehleha. vekane-llahu bikulli sey'in `alima
48|27|lekad sadeka-llahu rasulehu-rru'ya bilhakk. letedhulunne-lmescide-lharame in sae-llahu aminine muhallikine ruusekum vemukassirine la tehafun. fe`alime ma lem ta`lemu fece`ale min duni zalike fethan kariba
48|28|huve-llezi ersele rasulehu bilhuda vedini-lhakki liyuzhirahu `ale-ddini kullih. vekefa billahi sehida
48|29|muhammedur rasulu-llah. vellezine me`ahu esiddau `ale-lkuffari ruhamau beynehum terahum rukke`an succedey yebtegune fadlem mine-llahi veridvana. simahum fi vucuhihim min eseri-ssucud. zalike meseluhum fi-ttevrah. vemeseluhum fi-l'incil. kezer`in ahrace sat'ehu feazerahu festagleza festeva `ala sukihi yu`cibu-zzurra`a liyegiza bihimu-lkuffar. ve`ade-llahu-llezine amenu ve`amilu-ssalihati minhum magfiratev veecran `azima
49|1|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu la tukaddimu beyne yedeyi-llahi verasulihi vetteku-llah. inne-llahe semi`un `alim
49|2|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu la terfe`u asvatekum fevka savti-nnebiyyi vela techeru lehu bilkavli kecehri ba`dikum liba`din en tahbeta a`malukum veentum la tes`urun
49|3|inne-llezine yeguddune asvatehum `inde rasuli-llahi ulaike-llezine-mtehane-llahu kulubehum littakva. lehum magfiratuv veecrun `azim
49|4|inne-llezine yunaduneke miv verai-lhucurati ekseruhum la ya`kilun
49|5|velev ennehum saberu hatta tahruce ileyhim lekane hayral lehum. vellahu gafurur rahim
49|6|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu in caekum fasikum binebein fetebeyyenu en tusibu kavmem bicehaletin fetusbihu `ala ma fe`altum nadimin
49|7|va`lemu enne fikum rasule-llah. lev yuti`ukum fi kesirim mine-l'emri le`anittum velakinne-llahe habbebe ileykumu-l'imane vezeyyenehu fi kulubikum vekerrahe ileykumu-lkufra velfusuka vel`isyan. ulaike humu-rrasidun
49|8|fadlem mine-llahi veni`meh. vellahu `alimun hakim
49|9|vein taifetani mine-lmu'minine-ktetelu feaslihu beynehuma. feim begat ihdahuma `ale-l'uhra fekatilu-lleti tebgi hatta tefie ila emri-llah. fein faet feaslihu beynehuma bil`adli veaksitu. inne-llahe yuhibbu-lmuksitin
49|10|inneme-lmu'minune ihvetun feaslihu beyne ehaveykum vetteku-llahe le`allekum turhamun
49|11|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu la yeshar kavmum min kavmin `asa ey yekunu hayram minhum vela nisaum min nisain `asa ey yekunne hayram minhunn. vela telmizu enfusekum vela tenabezu bil'elkab. bi'se-lismu-lfusuku ba`de-l'iman. vemel lem yetub feulaike humu-zzalimun
49|12|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu-ctenibu kesiram mine-zzann. inne ba`da-zzanni ismuv vela tecessesu vela yagteb ba`dukum ba`da. eyuhibbu ehadukum ey ye'kule lahme ehihi meyten fekerihtumuh. vetteku-llah. inne-llahe tevvabur rahim
49|13|ya eyyuhe-nnasu inna halaknakum min zekeriv veunsa vece`alnakum su`ubev vekabaile lite`arafu. inne ekramekum `inde-llahi etkakum. inne-llahe `alimun habir
49|14|kaleti-l'a`rabu amenna. kul lem tu'minu velakin kulu eslemna velemma yedhuli-l'imanu fi kulubikum. vein tuti`u-llahe verasulehu la yelitkum min a`malikum sey'a. inne-llahe gafurur rahim
49|15|inneme-lmu'minune-llezine amenu billahi verasulihi summe lem yertabu vecahedu biemvalihim veenfusihim fi sebili-llah. ulaike humu-ssadikun
49|16|kul etu`allimune-llahe bidinikum vellahu ya`lemu ma fi-ssemavati vema fi-l'ard. vellahu bikulli sey'in `alim
49|17|yemunnune `aleyke en eslemu. kul la temunnu `aleyye islamekum. beli-llahu yemunnu `aleykum en hedakum lil'imani in kuntum sadikin

57|1|sebbeha lillahi ma fi-ssemavati vel'ard. vehuve-l`azizu-lhakim
57|2|lehu mulku-ssemavati vel'ard. yuhyi veyumit. vehuve `ala kulli sey'in kadir
57|3|huve-l'evvelu vel'ahiru vezzahiru velbatin. vehuve bikulli sey'in `alim
57|4|huve-llezi haleka-ssemavati vel'arda fi sitteti eyyamin summe-steva `ale-l`ars. ya`lemu ma yelicu fi-l'ardi vema yahrucu minha vema yenzilu mine-ssemai vema ya`rucu fiha. vehuve me`akum eyne ma kuntum. vellahu bima ta`melune besir
57|5|lehu mulku-ssemavati vel'ard. veile-llahi turce`u-l'umur
57|6|yulicu-lleyle fi-nnehari veyulicu-nnehara fi-lleyl. vehuve `alimum bizati-ssudur
57|7|aminu billahi verasulihi veenfiku mimma ce`alekum mustahlefine fih. fellezine amenu minkum veenfeku lehum ecrun kebir
57|8|vema lekum la tu'minune billah. verrasulu yed`ukum litu'minu birabbikum vekad ehaze misakakum in kuntum mu'minin
57|9|huve-llezi yunezzilu `ala `abdihi ayatim beyyinatil liyuhricekum mine-zzulumati ile-nnur. veinne-llahe bikum leraufur rahim
57|10|vema lekum ella tunfiku fi sebili-llahi velillahi mirasu-ssemavati vel'ard. la yestevi minkum men enfeka min kabli-lfethi vekatel. ulaike a`zamu deracetem mine-llezine enfeku mim ba`du vekatelu. vekullev ve`ade-llahu-lhusna. vellahu bima ta`melune habir
57|11|men ze-llezi yukridu-llahe kardan hasenen feyuda`ifehu lehu velehu ecrun kerim
57|12|yevme tera-lmu'minine velmu'minati yes`a nuruhum beyne eydihim vebieymanihim busrakumu-lyevme cennatun tecri min tahtihe-l'enharu halidine fiha. zalike huve-lfevzu-l`azim
57|13|yevme yekulu-lmunafikune velmunafikatu lillezine amenu-nzuruna naktebis min nurikum kile-rci`u veraekum feltemisu nura. feduribe beynehum bisuril lehu bab. batinuhu fihi-rrahmetu vezahiruhu min kibelihi-l`azab
57|14|yunadunehum elem nekum me`akum. kalu bela velakinnekum fetentum enfusekum veterabbastum vertebtum vegarratkumu-l'emaniyyu hatta cae emru-llahi vegarrakum billahi-lgarur
57|15|felyevme la yu'hazu minkum fidyetuv vela mine-llezine keferu. me'vakumu-nnar. hiye mevlakum. vebi'se-lmesir
57|16|elem ye'ni lillezine amenu en tahse`a kulubuhum lizikri-llahi vema nezele mine-lhakki vela yekunu kellezine utu-lkitabe min kablu fetale `aleyhimu-l'emedu fekaset kulubuhum. vekesirum minhum fasikun
57|17|i`lemu enne-llahe yuhyi-l'arda ba`de mevtiha. kad beyyenna lekumu-l'ayati le`allekum ta`kilun
57|18|inne-lmussaddikine velmussaddikati veakradu-llahe kardan haseney yuda`afu lehum velehum ecrun kerim
57|19|vellezine amenu billahi verusulihi ulaike humu-ssiddikun. vessuhedau `inde rabbihim. lehum ecruhum venuruhum. vellezine keferu vekezzebu biayatina ulaike ashabu-lcehim
57|20|i`lemu enneme-lhayatu-ddunya le`ibuv velehvuv vezinetuv vetefahurum beynekum vetekasurun fi-l'emvali vel'evlad. kemeseli gaysin a`cebe-lkuffara nebatuhu summe yehicu feterahu musferran summe yekunu hutama. vefi-l'ahirati `azabun sediduv vemagfiratum mine-llahi veridvan. veme-lhayatu-ddunya illa meta`u-lgurur
57|21|sabiku ila magfiratim mir rabbikum vecennetin `arduha ke`ardi-ssemai vel'ardi u`iddet lillezine amenu billahi verusulih. zalike fadlu-llahi yu'tihi mey yesa'. vellahu zu-lfadli-l`azim
57|22|ma esabe mim musibetin fi-l'ardi vela fi enfusikum illa fi kitabim min kabli en nebraeha. inne zalike `ale-llahi yesir
57|23|likeyla te'sev `ala ma fatekum vela tefrahu bima atakum. vellahu la yuhibbu kulle muhtalin fehur
57|24|ellezine yebhalune veye'murune-nnase bilbuhl. vemey yetevelle feinne-llahe huve-lganiyyu-lhamid
57|25|lekad erselna rusulena bilbeyyinati veenzelna me`ahumu-lkitabe velmizane liyekume-nnasu bilkist. veenzelne-lhadide fihi be'sun sediduv vemenafi`u linnasi veliya`leme-llahu mey yensuruhu verusulehu bilgayb. inne-llahe kaviyyun `aziz
57|26|velekad erselna nuhav veibrahime vece`alna fi zurriyyetihime-nnubuvvete velkitabe feminhum muhted. vekesirum minhum fasikun
57|27|summe kaffeyna `ala asarihim birusulina vekaffeyna bi`ise-bni meryeme veateynahu-l'incile vece`alna fi kulubi-llezine-ttebe`uhu ra'fetev verahmeh. verahbaniyyeten-btede`uha ma ketebnaha `aleyhim ille-btigae ridvani-llahi fema ra`avha hakka ri`ayetiha. feateyne-llezine amenu minhum ecrahum. vekesirum minhum fasikun
57|28|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu-tteku-llahe veaminu birasulihi yu'tikum kifleyni mir rahmetihi veyec`al lekum nuran temsune bihi veyagfir lekum. vellahu gafurur rahim
57|29|liella ya`leme ehlu-lkitabi ella yakdirune `ala sey'im min fadli-llahi veenne-lfadle biyedi-llahi yu'tihi mey yesa'. vellahu zu-lfadli-l`azim
58|1|kad semi`a-llahu kavle-lleti tucadiluke fi zevciha vetesteki ile-llah. vellahu yesme`u tehavurakuma. inne-llahe semi`um besir
58|2|ellezine yuzahirune minkum min nisaihim ma hunne ummehatihim. in ummehatuhum ille-llai velednahum. veinnehum leyekulune munkeram mine-lkavli vezura. veinne-llahe le`afuvvun gafur
58|3|vellezine yuzahirune min nisaihim summe ye`udune lima kalu fetahriru rakabetim min kabli ey yetemassa. zalikum tu`azune bih. vellahu bima ta`melune habir
58|4|femel lem yecid fesiyamu sehrayni mutetabi`ayni min kabli ey yetemassa. femel lem yesteti` feit`amu sittine miskina. zalike litu'minu billahi verasulih. vetilke hududu-llah. velilkafirine `azabun elim
58|5|inne-llezine yuhaddune-llahe verasulehu kubitu kema kubite-llezine min kablihim vekad enzelna ayatim beyyinat. velilkafirine `azabum muhin
58|6|yevme yeb`asuhumu-llahu cemi`an feyunebbiuhum bima `amilu. ahsahu-llahu venesuh. vellahu `ala kulli sey'in sehid
58|7|elem tera enne-llahe ya`lemu ma fi-ssemavati vema fi-l'ard. ma yekunu min necva selasetin illa huve rabi`uhum vela hamsetin illa huve sadisuhum vela edna min zalike vela eksera illa huve me`ahum eyne ma kanu. summe yunebbiuhum bima `amilu yevme-lkiyameh. inne-llahe bikulli sey'in `alim
58|8|elem tera ile-llezine nuhu `ani-nnecva summe ye`udune lima nuhu `anhu veyetenacevne bil'ismi vel`udvav vema`siyeti-rrasul. veiza cauke hayyevke bima lem yuhayyike bihi-llahu veyekulune fi enfusihim levla yu`azzibune-llahu bima nekul. hasbuhum cehennem. yaslevneha. febi'se-lmesir
58|9|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu iza tenaceytum fela tetenacev bil'ismi vel`udvani vema`siyeti-rrasuli vetenacev bilbirri vettakva. vetteku-llahe-llezi ileyhi tuhserun
58|10|inneme-nnecva mine-sseytani liyahzune-llezine amenu veleyse bidarrihim sey'en illa biizni-llah. ve`ale-llahi felyetevekkeli-lmu'minun
58|11|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu iza kile lekum tefessehu fi-lmecalisi fefsehu yefsehi-llahu lekum. veiza kile-nsuzu fensuzu yerfe`i-llahu-llezine amenu minkum vellezine utu-l`ilme deracat. vellahu bima ta`melune habir
58|12|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu iza naceytumu-rrasule fekaddimu beyne yedey necvakum sadekaten. zalike hayrul lekum veather. feil lem tecidu feinne-llahe gafurur rahim
58|13|eesfaktum en tukaddimu beyne yedey necvakum sadekat. feiz lem tef`alu vetabe-llahu `aleykum feekimu-ssalate veatu-zzekate veeti`u-llahe verasuleh. vellahu habirum bima ta`melun
58|14|elem tera ile-llezine tevellev kavmen gadibe-llahu `aleyhim. ma hum minkum vela minhum veyahlifune `ale-lkezibi vehum ya`lemun
58|15|e`adde-llahu lehum `azaben sedida. innehum sae ma kanu ya`melun
58|16|ittehazu eymanehum cunneten fesaddu `an sebili-llahi felehum `azabum muhin
58|17|len tugniye `anhum emvaluhum vela evladuhum mine-llahi sey'a. ulaike ashabu-nnar. hum fiha halidun
58|18|yevme yeb`asuhumu-llahu cemi`an feyahlifune lehu kema yahlifune lekum veyahsebune ennehum `ala sey'. ela innehum humu-lkazibun
58|19|istahveze `aleyhimu-sseytanu feensahum zikra-llah. ulaike hizbu-sseytan. ela inne hizbe-sseytani humu-lhasirun
58|20|inne-llezine yuhaddune-llahe verasulehu ulaike fi-l'ezellin
58|21|ketebe-llahu leaglibenne ene verusuli. inne-llahe kaviyyun `aziz
58|22|la tecidu kavmey yu'minune billahi velyevmi-l'ahiri yuvaddune men hadde-llahe verasulehu velev kanu abaehum ev ebnaehum ev ihvanehum ev `asiratehum. ulaike ketebe fi kulubihimu-l'imane veeyyedehum biruhim minh. veyudhiluhum cennatin tecri min tahtihe-l'enharu halidine fiha. radiye-llahu `anhum veradu `anh. ulaike hizbu-llah. ela inne hizbe-llahi humu-lmuflihun
59|1|sebbeha lillahi ma fi-ssemavati vema fi-l'ard. vehuve-l`azizu-lhakim
59|2|huve-llezi ahrace-llezine keferu min ehli-lkitabi min diyarihim lievveli-lhasr. ma zanentum ey yahrucu vezannu ennehum mani`atuhum husunuhum mine-llahi feetahumu-llahu min haysu lem yahtesibu vekazefe fi kulubihimu-rru`be yuhribune buyutehum bieydihim veeydi-lmu'minine fa`tebiru ya uli-l'ebsar
59|3|velevla en ketebe-llahu `aleyhimu-lcelae le`azzebehum fi-ddunya. velehum fi-l'ahirati `azabu-nnar
59|4|zalike biennehum sakku-llahe verasuleh. vemey yusakki-llahe feinne-llahe sedidu-l`ikab
59|5|ma kata`tum mil linetin ev teraktumuha kaimeten `ala usuliha febiizni-llahi veliyuhziye-lfasikin
59|6|vema efae-llahu `ala rasulihi minhum fema evceftum `aleyhi min hayliv vela rikabiv velakinne-llahe yusellitu rusulehu `ala mey yesa'. vellahu `ala kulli sey'in kadir
59|7|ma efae-llahu `ala rasulihi min ehli-lkura felillahi velirrasuli velizi-lkurba velyetama velmesakini vebni-ssebili key la yekune duletem beyne-l'agniyai minkum. vema atakumu-rrasulu fehuzuhu vema nehakum `anhu fentehu. vetteku-llah. inne-llahe sedidu-l`ikab
59|8|lilfukarai-lmuhacirine-llezine uhricu min diyarihim veemvalihim yebtegune fadlem mine-llahi veridvanev veyensurune-llahe verasuleh. ulaike humu-ssadikun
59|9|vellezine tebevveu-ddara vel'imane min kablihim yuhibbune men hacera ileyhim vela yecidune fi sudurihim hacetem mimma utu veyu'sirune `ala enfusihim velev kane bihim hasasah. vemey yuka suhha nefsihi feulaike humu-lmuflihun
59|10|vellezine cau mim ba`dihim yekulune rabbene-gfir lena veliihvanine-llezine sebekuna bil'imani vela tec`al fi kulubina gillel lillezine amenu rabbena inneke raufur rahim
59|11|elem tera ile-llezine nafeku yekulune liihvanihimu-llezine keferu min ehli-lkitabi lein uhrictum lenahrucenne me`akum vela nuti`u fikum ehaden ebedev vein kutiltum lenensurannekum. vellahu yeshedu innehum lekazibun
59|12|lein uhricu la yahrucune me`ahum. velein kutilu la yensurunehum. velein nesaruhum leyuvellunne-l'edbar. summe la yunsarun
59|13|leentum eseddu rahbeten fi sudurihim mine-llah. zalike biennehum kavmul la yefkahun
59|14|la yukatilunekum cemi`an illa fi kuram muhassanetin ev miv verai cudur. be'suhum beynehum sedid. tahsebuhum cemi`av vekulubuhum setta. zalike biennehum kavmul la ya`kilun
59|15|kemeseli-llezine min kablihim kariben zaku vebale emrihim. velehum `azabun elim
59|16|kemeseli-sseytani iz kale lil'insani-kfur. felemma kefera kale inni berium minke inni ehafu-llahe rabbe-l`alemin
59|17|fekane `akibetehuma ennehuma fi-nnari halideyni fiha. vezalike cezau-zzalimin
59|18|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu-tteku-llahe veltenzur nefsum ma kaddemet ligad. vetteku-llah. inne-llahe habirum bima ta`melun
59|19|vela tekunu kellezine nesu-llahe feensahum enfusehum. ulaike humu-lfasikun
59|20|la yestevi ashabu-nnari veashabu-lcenneh. ashabu-lcenneti humu-lfaizun
59|21|lev enzelna haze-lkur'ane `ala cebelil lera'eytehu hasi`am mutesaddi`am min hasyeti-llah. vetilke-l'emsalu nadribuha linnasi le`allehum yetefekkerun
59|22|huve-llahu-llezi la ilahe illa hu. `alimu-lgaybi vessehadeh. huve-rrahmanu-rrahim
59|23|huve-llahu-llezi la ilahe illa hu. elmeliku-lkuddusu-sselamu-lmu'minu-lmuheyminu-l`azizu-lcebbaru-lmutekebbir. subhane-llahi `amma yusrikun
59|24|huve-llahu-lhaliku-lbariu-lmusavviru lehu-l'esmau-lhusna. yusebbihu lehu ma fi-ssemavati vel'ard. vehuve-l`azizu-lhakim
60|1|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu la tettehizu `aduvvi ve`aduvvekum evliyae tulkune ileyhim bilmeveddeti vekad keferu bima caekum mine-lhakk. yuhricune-rrasule veiyyakum en tu'minu billahi rabbikum. in kuntum haractum cihaden fi sebili vebtigae merdati tusirrune ileyhim bilmeveddeh. veena a`lemu bima ahfeytum vema a`lentum. vemey yef`alhu minkum fekad dalle sevae-ssebil
60|2|iy yeskafukum yekunu lekum a`daev veyebsutu ileykum eydiyehum veelsinetehum bissui veveddu lev tekfurun
60|3|len tenfe`akum erhamukum vela evladukum. yevme-lkiyameh. yefsilu beynekum. vellahu bima ta`melune besir
60|4|kad kanet lekum usvetun hasenetun fi ibrahime vellezine me`ah. iz kalu likavmihim inna buraau minkum vemimma ta`budune min duni-llah. keferna bikum vebeda beynena vebeynekumu-l`adavetu vebagdau ebeden hatta tu'minu billahi vahdehu illa kavle ibrahime liebihi leestagfiranne leke vema emliku leke mine-llahi min sey'. rabbena `aleyke tevekkelna veileyke enebna veileyke-lmesir
60|5|rabbena la tec`alna fitnetel lillezine keferu vagfir lena rabbena. inneke ente-l`azizu-lhakim
60|6|lekad kane lekum fihim usvetun hasenetul limen kane yercu-llahe velyevme-l'ahir. vemey yetevelle feinne-llahe huve-lganiyyu-lhamid
60|7|asa-llahu ey yec`ale beynekum vebeyne-llezine `adeytum minhum meveddeh. vellahu kadir. vellahu gafurur rahim
60|8|la yenhakumu-llahu `ani-llezine lem yukatilukum fi-ddini velem yuhricukum min diyarikum en teberruhum vetuksitu ileyhim. inne-llahe yuhibbu-lmuksitin
60|9|innema yenhakumu-llahu `ani-llezine katelukum fi-ddini veahracukum min diyarikum vezaheru `ala ihracikum en tevellevhum. vemey yetevellehum feulaike humu-zzalimun
60|10|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu iza caekumu-lmu'minatu muhaciratin femtehinuhunn. allahu a`lemu biimanihinn. fein `alimtumuhunne mu'minatin fela terci`uhunne ile-lkuffar. la hunne hillul lehum vela hum yehillune lehunn. veatuhum ma enfeku. vela cunaha `aleykum en tenkihuhunne iza ateytumuhunne ucurahunn. vela tumsiku bi`isami-lkevafiri ves'elu ma enfaktum velyes'elu ma enfeku. zalikum hukmu-llah. yahkumu beynekum. vellahu `alimun hakim
60|11|vein fatekum sey'um min ezvacikum ile-lkuffari fe`akabtum featu-llezine zehebet ezvacuhum misle ma enfeku. vetteku-llahe-llezi entum bihi mu'minun
60|12|ya eyyuhe-nnebiyyu iza caeke-lmu'minatu yubayi`neke `ala el la yusrikne billahi sey'ev vela yesrikne vela yeznine vela yaktulne evladehunne vela ye'tine bibuhtaniy yefterinehu beyne eydihinne veerculihinne vela ya`sineke fi ma`rufin febayi`hunne vestagfir lehunne-llah. inne-llahe gafurur rahim
60|13|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu la tetevellev kavmen gadibe-llahu `aleyhim kad yeisu mine-l'ahirati kema yeise-lkuffaru min ashabi-lkubur
61|1|sebbeha lillahi ma fi-ssemavati vema fi-l'ard. vehuve-l`azizu-lhakim
61|2|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu lime tekulune ma la tef`alun
61|3|kebura makten `inde-llahi en tekulu ma la tef`alun
61|4|inne-llahe yuhibbu-llezine yukatilune fi sebilihi saffen keennehum bunyanum mersus
61|5|veiz kale musa likavmihi ya kavmi lime tu'zuneni vekat ta`lemune enni rasulu-llahi ileykum. felemma zagu ezaga-llahu kulubehum. vellahu la yehdi-lkavme-lfasikin
61|6|veiz kale `ise-bnu meryeme ya beni israile inni rasulu-llahi ileykum musaddikal lima beyne yedeyye mine-ttevrati vemubessiram birasuliy ye'ti mim ba`di-smuhu ahmed. felemma caehum bilbeyyinati kalu haza sihrum mubin
61|7|vemen azlemu mimmeni-ftera `ale-llahi-lkezibe vehuve yud`a ile-l'islam. vellahu la yehdi-lkavme-zzalimin
61|8|yuridune liyutfiu nura-llahi biefvahihim vellahu mutimmu nurihi velev kerihe-lkafirun
61|9|huve-llezi ersele rasulehu bilhuda vedini-lhakki liyuzhirahu `ale-ddini kullihi velev kerihe-lmusrikun
61|10|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu hel edullukum `ala ticaratin tuncikum min `azabin elim
61|11|tu'minune billahi verasulihi vetucahidune fi sebili-llahi biemvalikum veenfusikum. zalikum hayrul lekum in kuntum ta`lemun
61|12|yagfir lekum zunubekum veyudhilkum cennatin tecri min tahtihe-l'enharu vemesakine tayyibeten fi cennati `adn. zalike-lfevzu-l`azim
61|13|veuhra tuhibbuneha. nasrum mine-llahi vefethun karib. vebessiri-lmu'minin
61|14|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu kunu ensara-llahi kema kale `ise-bnu meryeme lilhavariyyine men ensari ile-llah. kale-lhavariyyune nahnu ensaru-llahi feamenet taifetum mim beni israile vekeferat taifeh. feeyyedne-llezine amenu `ala `aduvvihim feasbehu zahirin
62|1|yusebbihu lillahi ma fi-ssemavati vema fi-l'ardi-lmeliki-lkuddusi-l`azizi-lhakim
62|2|huve-llezi be`ase fi-l'ummiyyine rasulem minhum yetlu `aleyhim ayatihi veyuzekkihim veyu`allimuhumu-lkitabe velhikmeh. vein kanu min kablu lefi dalalim mubin
62|3|veaharine minhum lemma yelhaku bihim. vehuve-l`azizu-lhakim
62|4|zalike fadlu-llahi yu'tihi mey yesa'. vellahu zu-lfadli-l`azim
62|5|meselu-llezine hummilu-ttevrate summe lem yahmiluha kemeseli-lhimari yahmilu esfara. bi'se meselu-lkavmi-llezine kezzebu biayati-llah. vellahu la yehdi-lkavme-zzalimin
62|6|kul ya eyyuhe-llezine hadu in za`amtum ennekum evliyau lillahi min duni-nnasi fetemennevu-lmevte in kuntum sadikin
62|7|vela yetemennevnehu ebedem bima kaddemet eydihim. vellahu `alimum bizzalimin
62|8|kul inne-lmevte-llezi tefirrune minhu feinnehu mulakikum summe turaddune ila `alimi-lgaybi vessehadeti feyunebbiukum bima kuntum ta`melun
62|9|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu iza nudiye lissalati miy yevmi-lcumu`ati fes`av ila zikri-llahi vezeru-lbey`. zalikum hayrul lekum in kuntum ta`lemun
62|10|feiza kudiyeti-ssaletu fentesiru fi-l'ardi vebtegu min fadli-llahi vezkuru-llahe kesiral le`allekum tuflihun
62|11|veiza raev ticaraten ev lehven-nfeddu ileyha veterakuke kaima. kul ma `inde-llahi hayrum mine-llehvi vemine-tticarah. vellahu hayru-rrazikin
63|1|iza caeke-lmunafikune kalu neshedu inneke lerasulu-llah. vellahu ya`lemu inneke lerasuluh. vellahu yeshedu inne-lmunafikine lekazibun
63|2|ittehazu eymanehum cunneten fesaddu `an sebili-llah. innehum sae ma kanu ya`melun
63|3|zalike biennehum amenu summe keferu fetubi`a `ala kulubihim fehum la yefkahun
63|4|veiza raeytehum tu`cibuke ecsamuhum. veiy yekulu tesma` likavlihim. keennehum husubum musennedeh. yahsebune kulle sayhatin `aleyhim. humu-l`aduvvu fahzerhum. katelehumu-llah. enna yu'fekun
63|5|veiza kile lehum te`alev yestagfir lekum rasulu-llahi levvev ruusehum veraeytehum yesuddune vehum mustekbirun
63|6|sevaun `aleyhim estagferte lehum em lem testagfir lehum. ley yagfira-llahu lehum. inne-llahe la yehdi-lkavme-lfasikin
63|7|humu-llezine yekulune la tunfiku `ala men `inde rasuli-llahi hatta yenfeddu. velillahi hazainu-ssemavati vel'ardi velakinne-lmunafikine la yefkahun
63|8|yekulune leir raca`na ile-lmedineti leyuhricenne-l'e`azzu minhe-l'ezell. velillahi-l`izzetu velirasulihi velilmu'minine velakinne-lmunafikine la ya`lemun
63|9|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu la tulhikum emvalukum vela evladukum `an zikri-llah. vemey yef`al zalike feulaike humu-lhasirun
63|10|veenfiku mimma razaknakum min kabli ey ye'tiye ehadekumu-lmevtu feyekule rabbi levla ehharteni ila ecelin karibin feessaddeka veekum mine-ssalihin
63|11|veley yu'ehhira-llahu nefsen iza cae eceluha. vellahu habirum bima ta`melun
64|1|yusebbihu lillahi ma fi-ssemavati vema fi-l'ard. lehu-lmulku velehu-lhamd. vehuve `ala kulli sey'in kadir
64|2|huve-llezi halekakum feminkum kafiruv veminkum mu'min. vellahu bima ta`melune besir
64|3|haleka-ssemavati vel'arda bilhakki vesavverakum feahsene suverakum. veileyhi-lmesir
64|4|ya`lemu ma fi-ssemavati vel'ardi veya`lemu ma tusirrune vema tu`linun. vellahu `alimum bizati-ssudur
64|5|elem ye'tikum nebeu-llezine keferu min kabl. fezaku vebale emrihim velehum `azabun elim
64|6|zalike biennehu kanet te'tihim rusuluhum bilbeyyinati fekalu ebeseruy yehdunena. fekeferu vetevellev vestagne-llah. vellahu ganiyyun hamid
64|7|za`ame-llezine keferu el ley yub`asu. kul bela verabbi letub`asunne summe letunebbeunne bima `amiltum. vezalike `ale-llahi yesir
64|8|feaminu billahi verasulihi vennuri-llezi enzelna. vellahu bima ta`melune habir
64|9|yevme yecme`ukum liyevmi-lcem`i zalike yevmu-ttegabun. vemey yu'mim billahi veya`mel salihay yukeffir `anhu seyyiatihi veyudhilhu cennatin tecri min tahtihe-l'enharu halidine fiha ebeda. zalike-lfevzu-l`azim
64|10|vellezine keferu vekezzebu biayatina ulaike ashabu-nnari halidine fiha. vebi'se-lmesir
64|11|ma esabe mim musibetin illa biizni-llah. vemey yu'mim billahi yehdi kalbeh. vellahu bikulli sey'in `alim
64|12|veeti`u-llahe veeti`u-rrasul. fein tevelleytum feinnema `ala rasuline-lbelagu-lmubin
64|13|allahu la ilahe illa hu. ve`ale-llahi felyetevekkeli-lmu'minun
64|14|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu inne min ezvacikum veevladikum `aduvvel lekum fahzeruhum. vein ta`fu vetasfehu vetagfiru feinne-llahe gafurur rahim
64|15|innema emvalukum veevladukum fitnetun. vellahu `indehu ecrun `azim
64|16|fetteku-llahe me-steta`tum vesme`u veeti`u veenfiku hayral lienfusikum. vemey yuka suhha nefsihi feulaike humu-lmuflihun
64|17|in tukridu-llahe kardan haseney yuda`ifhu lekum veyagfir lekum. vellahu sekurun halim
64|18|alimu-lgaybi vessehadeti-l`azizu-lhakim
65|1|ya eyyuhe-nnebiyyu iza tallaktumu-nnisae fetallikuhunne li`iddetihinne veahsu-l`iddeh. vetteku-llahe rabbekum. la tuhricuhunne mim buyutihinne vela yahrucne illa ey ye'tine bifahisetim mubeyyineh. vetilke hududu-llah. vemey yete`adde hudude-llahi fekad zaleme nefseh. la tedri le`alle-llahe yuhdisu ba`de zalike emra
65|2|feiza belagne ecelehunne feemsikuhunne bima`rufin ev farikuhunne bima`rufiv veeshidu zevey `adlim minkum veekimu-ssehadete lillah. zalikum yu`azu bihi men kane yu'minu billahi velyevmi-l'ahir. vemey yetteki-llahe yec`al lehu mahraca
65|3|veyerzukhu min haysu la yahtesib. vemey yetevekkel `ale-llahi fehuve hasbuh. inne-llahe baligu emrih. kad ce`ale-llahu likulli sey'in kadra
65|4|vellai yeisne mine-lmehidi min nisaikum ini-rtebtum fe`iddetuhunne selasetu eshuriv vellai lem yehidn. veulatu-l'ahmali eceluhunne ey yeda`ne hamlehunn. vemey yetteki-llahe yec`al lehu min emrihi yusra
65|5|zalike emru-llahi enzelehu ileykum. vemey yetteki-llahe yukeffir `anhu seyyiatihi veyu`zim lehu ecra
65|6|eskinuhunne min haysu sekentum miv vucdikum vela tudarruhunne litudayyiku `aleyhinn. vein kunne ulati hamlin feenfiku `aleyhinne hatta yeda`ne hamlehunn. fein erda`ne lekum featuhunne ucurahunn. ve'temiru beynekum bima`ruf. vein te`asertum feseturdi`u lehu uhra
65|7|liyunfik zu se`atim min se`atih. vemen kudira `aleyhi rizkuhu felyunfik mimma atahu-llah. la yukellifu-llahu nefsen illa ma ataha. seyec`alu-llahu ba`de `usriy yusra
65|8|vekeeyyim min karyetin `atet `an emri rabbiha verusulihi fehasebnaha hisaben sedidev ve`azzebnaha `azaben nukra
65|9|fezakat vebale emriha vekane `akibetu emriha husra
65|10|e`adde-llahu lehum `azaben sediden fetteku-llahe ya uli-l'elbab. ellezine amenu. kad enzele-llahu ileykum zikra
65|11|rasuley yetlu `aleykum ayati-llahi mubeyyinatil liyuhrice-llezine amenu ve`amilu-ssalihati mine-zzulumati ile-nnur. vemey yu'mim billahi veya`mel salihay yudhilhu cennatin tecri min tahtihe-l'enharu halidine fiha ebeda. kad ahsene-llahu lehu rizka
65|12|allahu-llezi haleka seb`a semavativ vemine-l'ardi mislehunn. yetenezzelu-l'emru beynehunne lita`lemu enne-llahe `ala kulli sey'in kadiruv veenne-llahe kad ehata bikulli sey'in `ilma
66|1|ya eyyuhe-nnebiyyu lime tuharrimu ma ehalle-llahu leke. tebtegi merdate ezvacik. vellahu gafurur rahim
66|2|kad ferada-llahu lekum tehillete eymanikum. vellahu mevlakum. vehuve-l`alimu-lhakim
66|3|veiz eserra-nnebiyyu ila ba`di ezvacihi hadisa. felemma nebbeet bihi veazherahu-llahu `aleyhi `arrafe ba`dahu vea`rada `am ba`d. felemma nebbeeha bihi kalet men embeeke haza. kale nebbeeniye-l`alimu-lhabir
66|4|in tetuba ile-llahi fekad sagat kulubukuma. vein tezahera `aleyhi feinne-llahe huve mevlahu vecibrilu vesalihu-lmu'minin. velmelaiketu ba`de zalike zahir
66|5|asa rabbuhu in tallekakunne ey yubdilehu ezvacen hayram minkunne muslimatim mu'minatin kanitatin taibatin `abidatin saihatin seyyibativ veebkara
66|6|ya eyyuhe-llezine amenu ku enfusekum veehlikum narav vekuduhe-nnasu velhicaratu `aleyha melaiketun gilazun sidadul la ya`sune-llahe ma emerahum veyef`alune ma yu'merun
66|7|ya eyyuhe-llezine keferu la ta`teziru-lyevm. innema tuczevne ma kuntum ta`melun
